style=\"color:#f6c65b\">Course Home<\/a> | <a href=\"\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-1-welcome-to-the-live-event-world\/\" style=\"color:#f6c65b\">Module 1<\/a><\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"32px\"} --><div style=\"height:32px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:group {\"style\":{\"border\":{\"color\":\"#303846\",\"width\":\"1px\",\"radius\":\"20px\"},\"color\":{\"background\":\"#141820\"},\"spacing\":{\"padding\":{\"top\":\"40px\",\"bottom\":\"40px\",\"left\":\"40px\",\"right\":\"40px\"}}},\"layout\":{\"type\":\"constrained\"}} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-group has-border-color has-background\" style=\"border-color:#303846;border-width:1px;border-radius:20px;background-color:#141820;padding:40px\">\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"26px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:26px;font-weight:800\">What You Will Learn<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:list {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"}}} -->\n<ul style=\"color:#c6c8cc\"><li>The main roles on a live event crew<\/li><li>The difference between touring crew, local crew, and house crew<\/li><li>Who you report to and why the chain of command matters<\/li><li>How departments work together to make a show happen<\/li><\/ul>\n<!-- \/wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"24px\"} --><div style=\"height:24px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"26px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:26px;font-weight:800\">The Crew Is a Team<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\">Live event production requires many people working in coordination. Understanding who is on the crew helps you know who to listen to, who to ask for help, and how your role fits into the larger picture.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"22px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:22px;font-weight:800\">Touring Crew vs. Local Crew<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\">The <strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">touring crew<\/strong> travels with the production and knows the show inside and out. The <strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">local crew<\/strong> is hired in each city to provide labor and works under touring crew direction. Some venues also have a <strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">house crew<\/strong> employed by the venue for building-specific operations.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"22px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:22px;font-weight:800\">Key Crew Roles<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Production Manager:<\/strong> Oversees the entire production - schedule, budget, and coordination of all departments.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Department Heads:<\/strong> Each technical department has a head responsible for that department's work and crew direction.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Steward or Key:<\/strong> In union environments, the steward manages crew assignments and jurisdiction. The key is the lead stagehand for a department.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Stagehands (Local Labor):<\/strong> Assigned to departments based on the needs of the call. Show up ready, pay attention, and execute.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"22px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:22px;font-weight:800\">The Chain of Command<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\">You report to your department lead or key. Your lead reports to the department head. Department heads coordinate with the production manager. Decisions flow down. Questions flow up. As a new stagehand, your job is to understand this structure, work within it, and build trust. That is how you get called back.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"24px\"} --><div style=\"height:24px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:group {\"style\":{\"border\":{\"color\":\"#f6c65b\",\"width\":\"1px\",\"radius\":\"12px\"},\"color\":{\"background\":\"#1a1600\"},\"spacing\":{\"padding\":{\"top\":\"20px\",\"bottom\":\"20px\",\"left\":\"24px\",\"right\":\"24px\"}}},\"layout\":{\"type\":\"constrained\"}} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-group has-border-color has-background\" style=\"border-color:#f6c65b;border-width:1px;border-radius:12px;background-color:#1a1600;padding:20px 24px\">\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f6c65b\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"12px\",\"fontWeight\":\"900\",\"letterSpacing\":\"0.1em\",\"textTransform\":\"uppercase\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#f6c65b;font-size:12px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase\">Key Takeaway<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"16px\",\"lineHeight\":\"1.65\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:16px;line-height:1.65\">Know the difference between touring, local, and house crew. Understand your chain of command. As a new stagehand, you are local crew - report to your lead, work within the production structure, and build trust through consistent professional work.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<\/div>\n<!-- \/wp:group -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"40px\"} --><div style=\"height:40px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:buttons -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-buttons\"><div class=\"wp-block-button\"><a class=\"wp-block-button__link wp-element-button\" href=\"\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-1-welcome-to-the-live-event-world\/lesson-1-5-what-makes-a-new-stagehand-valuable\/\" style=\"border-radius:999px;background-color:#f6c65b;color:#101010;font-weight:800\">Next Lesson: What Makes a New Stagehand Valuable<\/a><\/div><\/div>\n<!-- \/wp:buttons -->\n\n<\/div>\n<!-- \/wp:group -->\n<\/div>\n<!-- \/wp:group -->","excerpt":""}}{"data":{"id":325,"status":"publish","type":"page","date":"2026-05-25T14:13:58","modified":"2026-05-25T14:13:58","link":"https:\/\/thecrewblueprint.wpcomstaging.com\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-1-welcome-to-the-live-event-world\/lesson-1-5-what-makes-a-new-stagehand-valuable\/","author":280519757,"parent":320,"menu_order":0,"template":"","featured_media":0,"comment_status":"closed","meta":{"_crdt_document":"","advanced_seo_description":"","jetpack_seo_html_title":"","jetpack_seo_noindex":false,"footnotes":"","_yoast_wpseo_title":"","_yoast_wpseo_metadesc":"","_yoast_wpseo_focuskw":"","rank_math_title":"","rank_math_description":"","rank_math_focus_keyword":"","_aioseop_title":"","_aioseop_description":""},"title":"Lesson 1.5: What Makes a New Stagehand Valuable","content":"<!-- wp:group {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"background\":\"#0b0d10\"}},\"className\":\"alignfull\",\"layout\":{\"type\":\"constrained\"}} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-group alignfull has-background\" style=\"background-color:#0b0d10;padding-top:60px;padding-bottom:80px;padding-left:24px;padding-right:24px\">\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f6c65b\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"13px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\",\"letterSpacing\":\"0.12em\",\"textTransform\":\"uppercase\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#f6c65b;font-size:13px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:0.12em;text-transform:uppercase\">Module 1 - Lesson 1.5<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":1,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"44px\",\"fontWeight\":\"900\",\"letterSpacing\":\"-0.04em\"}}} -->\n<h1 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:44px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:-0.04em\">What Makes a New Stagehand Valuable<\/h1>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"14px\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;font-size:14px\"><a href=\"\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/\" style=\"color:#f6c65b\">Course Home<\/a> | <a href=\"\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-1-welcome-to-the-live-event-world\/\" style=\"color:#f6c65b\">Module 1<\/a><\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"32px\"} --><div style=\"height:32px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:group {\"style\":{\"border\":{\"color\":\"#303846\",\"width\":\"1px\",\"radius\":\"20px\"},\"color\":{\"background\":\"#141820\"},\"spacing\":{\"padding\":{\"top\":\"40px\",\"bottom\":\"40px\",\"left\":\"40px\",\"right\":\"40px\"}}},\"layout\":{\"type\":\"constrained\"}} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-group has-border-color has-background\" style=\"border-color:#303846;border-width:1px;border-radius:20px;background-color:#141820;padding:40px\">\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"26px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:26px;font-weight:800\">What You Will Learn<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:list {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"}}} -->\n<ul style=\"color:#c6c8cc\"><li>What experienced crew members actually want from a new stagehand<\/li><li>The behaviors and habits that get you called back<\/li><li>The attitudes and actions that will end your career before it starts<\/li><li>How to build a reputation that opens doors<\/li><\/ul>\n<!-- \/wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"24px\"} --><div style=\"height:24px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"26px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:26px;font-weight:800\">It Is Not About What You Know Yet<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\">Nobody expects a new stagehand to know everything. You are new. That is understood. What experienced crew members do expect is that you show up on time, pay attention, work hard, and behave professionally. The skills come with time. The attitude has to be there from day one.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"22px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:22px;font-weight:800\">What Gets You Called Back<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Show up on time.<\/strong> Early is on time. On time is late. If your call is at 8:00 AM, you should be ready to work at 8:00 AM, not walking through the door. This is not negotiable.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Stay off your phone.<\/strong> Your phone should be in your pocket. Not in your hand. Not in front of your face. If you are on your phone when there is work to do, you will be noticed - and not in a good way.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Find the work.<\/strong> When you finish a task, do not stand around waiting to be told what to do next. Look around. Find something that needs to be done and either do it or ask your lead if that is the right next step.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Take direction without argument.<\/strong> This is not the time to explain why you think something should be done differently. If you have a safety concern, raise it. Otherwise, do the work the way you are asked to do it.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Treat the equipment well.<\/strong> Do not drag cases. Do not drop gear. Do not lean on things that are not meant to hold weight. Equipment is expensive and sometimes irreplaceable. Handle everything like it matters - because it does.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Ask questions the right way.<\/strong> Asking questions is good. Asking the same question multiple times because you were not paying attention the first time is not. When you get instructions, listen carefully. If something is unclear, ask for clarification right then - not after you have already done it wrong.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\"><strong style=\"color:#f7f7f2\">Be reliable.<\/strong> If you say you will be there, be there. If something comes up and you cannot make a call, give as much notice as possible and communicate clearly. Ghosting a call is one of the fastest ways to burn a bridge in this industry.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"22px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:22px;font-weight:800\">What Ends Careers Early<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\">The live event industry is smaller than it looks. Word travels fast. Being late, being unreliable, being difficult to work with, or having a bad attitude will follow you. So will being known as someone who does not work safely, does not listen, or does not take the job seriously. Protect your reputation from day one.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"22px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:22px;font-weight:800\">Your Reputation Is Your Resume<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"lineHeight\":\"1.75\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;line-height:1.75\">In live event production, most work comes through word of mouth and personal referral. The crew member who vouches for you is putting their own reputation on the line. Earn that trust by being someone worth vouching for. Every call is an interview for the next one.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"24px\"} --><div style=\"height:24px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:group {\"style\":{\"border\":{\"color\":\"#f6c65b\",\"width\":\"1px\",\"radius\":\"12px\"},\"color\":{\"background\":\"#1a1600\"},\"spacing\":{\"padding\":{\"top\":\"20px\",\"bottom\":\"20px\",\"left\":\"24px\",\"right\":\"24px\"}}},\"layout\":{\"type\":\"constrained\"}} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-group has-border-color has-background\" style=\"border-color:#f6c65b;border-width:1px;border-radius:12px;background-color:#1a1600;padding:20px 24px\">\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f6c65b\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"12px\",\"fontWeight\":\"900\",\"letterSpacing\":\"0.1em\",\"textTransform\":\"uppercase\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#f6c65b;font-size:12px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase\">Key Takeaway<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"16px\",\"lineHeight\":\"1.65\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:16px;line-height:1.65\">New stagehands are not expected to know everything. They are expected to show up on time, work hard, stay off their phones, take direction, and be reliable. Skills are learned. Attitude and professionalism are required from day one. Every call is an interview for the next one.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<\/div>\n<!-- \/wp:group -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"40px\"} --><div style=\"height:40px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:buttons -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-buttons\"><div class=\"wp-block-button\"><a class=\"wp-block-button__link wp-element-button\" href=\"\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-1-welcome-to-the-live-event-world\/\" style=\"border-radius:999px;background-color:#303846;color:#f7f7f2;font-weight:800\">Back to Module 1<\/a><\/div><div class=\"wp-block-button\"><a class=\"wp-block-button__link wp-element-button\" href=\"\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-1-welcome-to-the-live-event-world\/module-1-quiz\/\" style=\"border-radius:999px;background-color:#f6c65b;color:#101010;font-weight:800\">Take the Module 1 Quiz<\/a><\/div><\/div>\n<!-- \/wp:buttons -->\n\n<\/div>\n<!-- \/wp:group -->\n<\/div>\n<!-- \/wp:group -->","excerpt":""}}Module 1 fully built ✓ — all 5 lessons live. Now building Module 2 and its 7 lessons. Starting with the Module 2 index page:{"data":{"id":326,"status":"publish","type":"page","date":"2026-05-25T14:14:58","modified":"2026-05-25T14:14:58","link":"https:\/\/thecrewblueprint.wpcomstaging.com\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-2-safety-mindset-before-skillset\/","author":280519757,"parent":54,"menu_order":0,"template":"","featured_media":0,"comment_status":"closed","meta":{"_crdt_document":"","advanced_seo_description":"","jetpack_seo_html_title":"","jetpack_seo_noindex":false,"footnotes":"","_yoast_wpseo_title":"","_yoast_wpseo_metadesc":"","_yoast_wpseo_focuskw":"","rank_math_title":"","rank_math_description":"","rank_math_focus_keyword":"","_aioseop_title":"","_aioseop_description":""},"title":"Module 2: Safety Mindset Before Skillset","content":"<!-- wp:group {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"background\":\"#0b0d10\"}},\"className\":\"alignfull\",\"layout\":{\"type\":\"constrained\"}} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-group alignfull has-background\" style=\"background-color:#0b0d10;padding-top:60px;padding-bottom:60px;padding-left:24px;padding-right:24px\">\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f6c65b\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"13px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\",\"letterSpacing\":\"0.12em\",\"textTransform\":\"uppercase\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#f6c65b;font-size:13px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:0.12em;text-transform:uppercase\">Stagehand Fundamentals - Module 02<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":1,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"48px\",\"fontWeight\":\"900\",\"letterSpacing\":\"-0.04em\"}}} -->\n<h1 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:48px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:-0.04em\">Safety Mindset Before Skillset<\/h1>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"19px\",\"lineHeight\":\"1.65\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;font-size:19px;line-height:1.65\">Learn why safety comes before speed on a live event jobsite, understand your rights and responsibilities as a worker, and build the professional habits that protect you and your crew.<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#c6c8cc\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"14px\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#c6c8cc;font-size:14px\">7 Lessons | End-of-Module Quiz | <a href=\"\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/\" style=\"color:#f6c65b\">Back to Course<\/a><\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:spacer {\"height\":\"40px\"} --><div style=\"height:40px\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"wp-block-spacer\"><\/div><!-- \/wp:spacer -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":2,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"28px\",\"fontWeight\":\"900\"}}} -->\n<h2 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:28px;font-weight:900\">Lessons<\/h2>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:group {\"style\":{\"border\":{\"color\":\"#303846\",\"width\":\"1px\",\"radius\":\"16px\"},\"color\":{\"background\":\"#141820\"},\"spacing\":{\"padding\":{\"top\":\"24px\",\"bottom\":\"24px\",\"left\":\"24px\",\"right\":\"24px\"}}},\"layout\":{\"type\":\"constrained\"}} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-group has-border-color has-background\" style=\"border-color:#303846;border-width:1px;border-radius:16px;background-color:#141820;padding:24px\">\n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f6c65b\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"12px\",\"fontWeight\":\"900\",\"letterSpacing\":\"0.1em\",\"textTransform\":\"uppercase\"}}} -->\n<p style=\"color:#f6c65b;font-size:12px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase\">Lesson 2.1<\/p>\n<!-- \/wp:paragraph -->\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"style\":{\"color\":{\"text\":\"#f7f7f2\"},\"typography\":{\"fontSize\":\"20px\",\"fontWeight\":\"800\"}}} -->\n<h3 style=\"color:#f7f7f2;font-size:20px;font-weight:800\">Why Safety Comes Before Speed<\/h3>\n<!-- \/wp:heading -->\n<!-- wp:buttons -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-buttons\"><div class=\"wp-block-button is-style-outline\"><a class=\"wp-block-button__link wp-element-button\" href=\"\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-2-safety-mindset-before-skillset\/lesson-2-1-why-safety-comes-before-speed\/\" "req_011CbQgtojf6f6iJ3YcNYfVA"}{"data":{"id":327,"status":"publish","type":"page","date":"2026-05-25T23:15:07","modified":"2026-05-25T23:15:07","link":"https:\/\/thecrewblueprint.wpcomstaging.com\/general-site\/stagehand-fundamentals\/module-2-safety-mindset-before-skillset\/lesson-2-1-why-safety-comes-before-speed\/","author":280519757,"parent":326,"menu_order":0,"template":"","featured_media":0,"comment_status":"closed","meta":{"_crdt_document":"","advanced_seo_description":"","jetpack_seo_html_title":"","jetpack_seo_noindex":false,"footnotes":""},"title":"Lesson 2.1: Why Safety Comes Before Speed","content":"<!-- wp:group {\"style\":{\"color\":{\"background\":\"#0b0d10\"}},\"className\":\"alignfull\",\"layout\":{\"type\":\"constrained\"}} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-group alignfull has-background\" style=\"background-color:#0b0d10;padding-top:60px;padding-bottom:80px;padding-left:24px;padding-right:24px\">\n<!-- wp:paragraph
